https://ichef.bbci.co.uk/ace/standard/320/cpsprodpb/503D/production/_92614502_hi036530794.jpg 320w, https://ichef.bbci.co.uk/ace/standard/480/cpsprodpb/503D/production/_92614502_hi036530794.jpg 480w, https://ichef.bbci.co.uk/ace/standard/624/cpsprodpb/503D/production/_92614502_hi036530794.jpg 624w, https://ichef.bbci.co.uk/ace/standard/800/cpsprodpb/503D/production/_92614502_hi036530794.jpg 800w, https://ichef.bbci.co.uk/ace/standard/976/cpsprodpb/503D/production/_92614502_hi036530794.jpg 976w" width="976"/></picture></span><span class="ssrcss-2z7a81-StyledFigureCopyright e34k3c20" role="text"><span class="visually-hidden ssrcss-1f39n02-VisuallyHidden e16en2lz0">Image source, </span>Reuters</span></div></figure></div><div class="ssrcss-suhx0k-RichTextComponentWrapper ep2nwvo0" data-component="text-block"><div class="ssrcss-1o5p6v2-RichTextContainer e5tfeyi1"><p class="ssrcss-1q0x1qg-Paragraph e1jhz7w10"><b class="ssrcss-1xjjfut-BoldText e5tfeyi3">Donald Trump's extensive, international business holdings mean he will have to make decisions as leader of the US that also affect his businesses. Here's a look at some of his potential conflicts of interest.</b></p><p class="ssrcss-1q0x1qg-Paragraph e1jhz7w10">The Trump Organization is an umbrella company for Donald Trump's hundreds of investments in real estate, brands and other businesses. </p><p class="ssrcss-1q0x1qg-Paragraph e1jhz7w10">As head of the executive branch and a business owner, he has the ability to influence both US policy and government agencies to benefit his bottom line. </p><p class="ssrcss-1q0x1qg-Paragraph e1jhz7w10">Presidents are not subject to the same conflict of interest rules as other government employees, but previous commanders-in-chief have placed their investments into a blind trust to prevent any question of corruption.</p><p class="ssrcss-1q0x1qg-Paragraph e1jhz7w10">Ahead of the inauguration, Mr Trump placed his business holdings in a revocable trust managed by his two adult sons, Eric and Donald Jr. But while this removes him from the day-to-day decision making of his business, the president still retains a long-term interest in making sure his companies are doing well. </p><p class="ssrcss-1q0x1qg-Paragraph e1jhz7w10">Eric Trump told <a class="ssrcss-f6h2dj-InlineLink e1kn3p7n0" href="https://www.forbes.com/sites/danalexander/2017/03/24/after-promising-not-donald-talk-business-with-father-eric-trump-says-president-give-him-financial-reports/#15b87694359a">Forbes in March<span class="visually-hidden ssrcss-1f39n02-VisuallyHidden e16en2lz0">, <!-- -->external</span></a> he may share quarterly reports with his father, despite a statement that they would not discuss business or government with each other. Shortly after, <a class="ssrcss-f6h2dj-InlineLink e1kn3p7n0" href="https://www.propublica.org/article/trump-pull-money-his-businesses-whenever-he-wants-without-telling-us">ProPublica reported<span class="visually-hidden ssrcss-1f39n02-VisuallyHidden e16en2lz0">, <!-- -->external</span></a> Mr Trump could draw money from the trust at any time, without external disclosure.</p><p class="ssrcss-1q0x1qg-Paragraph e1jhz7w10">Ethics experts have urged Mr Trump to liquidate his business holdings so that he can avoid any appearance of a conflict, as the public nature of most of his businesses means it impossible to prevent him from knowing how government policies will affect his bottom line.</p></div></div><div class="ssrcss-suhx0k-RichTextComponentWrapper ep2nwvo0" data-component="text-block"><div class="ssrcss-1o5p6v2-RichTextContainer e5tfeyi1"><div class="ssrcss-h5qd1q-ListContainer e5tfeyi0"><ul role="list"><li><p class="ssrcss-1q0x1qg-Paragraph e1jhz7w10">Read more here about <a class="ssrcss-f6h2dj-InlineLink e1kn3p7n0" href="/news/business-38070411">how the Trump Organization's business works and what it means for the presidency</a>. </p></li></ul></div></div></div><div class="ssrcss-suhx0k-RichTextComponentWrapper ep2nwvo0" data-component="text-block"><div class="ssrcss-1o5p6v2-RichTextContainer e5tfeyi1"><p class="ssrcss-1q0x1qg-Paragraph e1jhz7w10">Below is a list of known conflicts of interest for Mr Trump, both foreign and domestic. Because his business is private, the full extent of his holdings - and the potential for conflicts - is not known. </p></div></div><div class="ssrcss-10wcwg8-ComponentWrapper-FullWidthWrapper ep2nwvo1" data-component="image-block"><figure class="ssrcss-12gl1u2-StyledFigure e34k3c22"><div class="ssrcss-ab5fd8-StyledFigureContainer e34k3c21"><span class="ssrcss-ciorxc-Placeholder class="ssrcss-1o1fzgd-ComponentWrapper-HeadlineComponentWrapper egtrm1f0" data-component="subheadline-block"><h2 class="ssrcss-pbttu9-Heading e10rt3ze0" id="American-conflicts-of-interest" tabindex="-1"><span role="text">American conflicts of interest</span></h2></div><div class="ssrcss-suhx0k-RichTextComponentWrapper ep2nwvo0" data-component="text-block"><div class="ssrcss-1o5p6v2-RichTextContainer e5tfeyi1"><p class="ssrcss-1q0x1qg-Paragraph e1jhz7w10"><b class="ssrcss-1xjjfut-BoldText e5tfeyi3">Trump International Hotel</b></p></div></div><div class="ssrcss-10wcwg8-ComponentWrapper-FullWidthWrapper ep2nwvo1" data-component="image-block"><figure class="ssrcss-12gl1u2-StyledFigure e34k3c22"><div class="ssrcss-ab5fd8-StyledFigureContainer (C) and his family prepare to cut the ribbon at the new Trump International Hotel in October 2016</p></div></figcaption></figure></div><div class="ssrcss-suhx0k-RichTextComponentWrapper ep2nwvo0" data-component="text-block"><div class="ssrcss-1o5p6v2-RichTextContainer e5tfeyi1"><p class="ssrcss-1q0x1qg-Paragraph e1jhz7w10">The Trump Organization leases the Old Post Office Building from US government's General Services Administration (GSA) for the Trump International Hotel in Washington, DC.Trump as president is both "landlord and tenant" of this building, says Steven Schooner, who along with Daniel Gordon, has <a class="ssrcss-f6h2dj-InlineLink e1kn3p7n0" href="https://www.washingtonpost.com/posteverything/wp/2016/11/15/trump-needs-to-give-up-his-trump-hotel-lease-right-now/?utm_term=.ab28c6e9dcb8">called on Trump to end the lease<span class="visually-hidden ssrcss-1f39n02-VisuallyHidden e16en2lz0">, <!-- -->external</span></a>.</p><p class="ssrcss-1q0x1qg-Paragraph e1jhz7w10">The 60-year lease will likely involve renegotiations - and the person responsible for setting the rent prices would ultimately report to the head of the GSA, a Trump appointee.In addition, the lease bars any federal employee, including elected officials, from benefitting from contracts with the government.</p><p class="ssrcss-1q0x1qg-Paragraph e1jhz7w10">But in a March letter, the GSA said it had determined Mr Trump was in "full compliance" with the lease because his interests in the hotel had been placed in a revocable trust, which he would see no personal benefit from during his term in office. </p><p class="ssrcss-1q0x1qg-Paragraph e1jhz7w10">The letter was written by the GSA employee who had done the initial negotiations over the building.</p><p class="ssrcss-1q0x1qg-Paragraph e1jhz7w10">The letter has not stopped criticism.</p><p class="ssrcss-1q0x1qg-Paragraph e1jhz7w10">"Donald Trump still owns the hotel, still will benefit from payments and still has a vested interest in its success," Noah Bookbinder, executive director of Citizens for Responsibility and Ethics in Washington, told CNN. Bookbinder's organisation sued Mr Trump shortly after he was sworn in over foreign conflicts of interests.</p><p class="ssrcss-1q0x1qg-Paragraph e1jhz7w10">Meanwhile, the hotel has already been <a class="ssrcss-f6h2dj-InlineLink e1kn3p7n0" href="https://www.washingtonpost.com/business/capitalbusiness/2016/11/18/9da9c572-ad18-11e6-977a-1030f822fc35_story.html">pitched to foreign diplomats<span class="visually-hidden ssrcss-1f39n02-VisuallyHidden e16en2lz0">, <!-- -->external</span></a> as a place to stay while in Washington, raising concerns that foreign governments could see booking expensive rooms at the Trump International as a way to gain favour with the Trump administration.</p></div></div><div class="ssrcss-10wcwg8-ComponentWrapper-FullWidthWrapper ep2nwvo1" data-component="image-block"><figure class="ssrcss-12gl1u2-StyledFigure e34k3c22"><div class="ssrcss-ab5fd8-StyledFigureContainer e34k3c21"><span class="ssrcss-ciorxc-Placeholder ep2nwvo0" data-component="text-block"><div class="ssrcss-1o5p6v2-RichTextContainer e5tfeyi1"><p class="ssrcss-1q0x1qg-Paragraph e1jhz7w10">The Trump Organization owns the right to lease the space in this office building in Manhattan - and makes money from the rent paid to the building. </p><p class="ssrcss-1q0x1qg-Paragraph e1jhz7w10"><a class="ssrcss-f6h2dj-InlineLink e1kn3p7n0" href="https://www.bloomberg.com/graphics/2016-trump-40-wall-street/">According to Bloomberg News<span class="visually-hidden ssrcss-1f39n02-VisuallyHidden e16en2lz0">, <!-- -->external</span></a>, there are five ongoing federal investigations into current or former tenants of 40 Wall Street, mostly for securities fraud. </p><p class="ssrcss-1q0x1qg-Paragraph e1jhz7w10">Those investigations are headed up by the Securities and Exchange Commission (SEC). </p><p class="ssrcss-1q0x1qg-Paragraph e1jhz7w10">Mr Trump's appointee to head the SEC, Jay Clayton, has been criticised for his ties to Wall Street firms by Democrats during his confirmation hearings.</p></div></div><div id="piano-inline1"></div><div class="ssrcss-10wcwg8-ComponentWrapper-FullWidthWrapper ep2nwvo1" ep2nwvo0" data-component="text-block"><div class="ssrcss-1o5p6v2-RichTextContainer e5tfeyi1"><p class="ssrcss-1q0x1qg-Paragraph e1jhz7w10">Sioux tribes and allies had <a class="ssrcss-f6h2dj-InlineLink e1kn3p7n0" href="/news/world-us-canada-37863955">protesting for months</a> to prevent the Dakota Access pipeline from being built under water supplies near the Standing Rock reservation. </p><p class="ssrcss-1q0x1qg-Paragraph e1jhz7w10">Trump had a partial investment - somewhere between $500,000 and $1m - in the <a class="ssrcss-f6h2dj-InlineLink e1kn3p7n0" href="http://abcnews.go.com/Politics/donald-trump-invested-company-controversial-dakota-access-pipeline/story?id=42748326">parent company of the firm<span class="visually-hidden ssrcss-1f39n02-VisuallyHidden e16en2lz0">, <!-- -->external</span></a> building Dakota Access pipeline, Energy Transfers Partners. </p><p class="ssrcss-1q0x1qg-Paragraph e1jhz7w10">Trump campaign spokeswoman Hope Hicks says Mr Trump has sold his stock in Energy Transfer Partners. But another one of Trump's stock holdings, Phillips 66, owns a 25% <a class="ssrcss-f6h2dj-InlineLink e1kn3p7n0" href="http://www.cbsnews.com/news/donald-trumps-stock-in-dakota-access-oil-pipeline-raises-concerns/">share in the project<span class="visually-hidden ssrcss-1f39n02-VisuallyHidden e16en2lz0">, <!-- -->external</span></a>. </p><p class="ssrcss-1q0x1qg-Paragraph e1jhz7w10">It's unclear if the president has also sold his stock in Phillips 66, as his last financial disclosure was in May 2016.</p><p class="ssrcss-1q0x1qg-Paragraph e1jhz7w10"><b class="ssrcss-1xjjfut-BoldText e5tfeyi3">Update:</b></p><p class="ssrcss-1q0x1qg-Paragraph e1jhz7w10">On 24 January, Mr Trump signed an executive order paving the way for final construction of the pipeline. ETP began work in early February and oil is expected to flow by early April. The pipeline remains the subject of a lawsuit by the Cheyenne River Sioux.</p></div></div><div class="ssrcss-10wcwg8-ComponentWrapper-FullWidthWrapper ep2nwvo1" data-component="image-block"><figure class="ssrcss-12gl1u2-StyledFigure e34k3c22"><div class="ssrcss-ab5fd8-StyledFigureContainer e34k3c21"><span class="ssrcss-ciorxc-Placeholder etlorgc0"><picture><source srcset="https://ichef.bbci.co.uk/ace/standard/240/mcs/media/images/75306000/jpg/_75306515_line976.jpg.webp 240w, class="ssrcss-1o1fzgd-ComponentWrapper-HeadlineComponentWrapper egtrm1f0" data-component="subheadline-block"><h2 class="ssrcss-pbttu9-Heading e10rt3ze0" id="Deutsche-Bank" tabindex="-1"><span role="text">Deutsche Bank</span></h2></div><div class="ssrcss-suhx0k-RichTextComponentWrapper ep2nwvo0" data-component="text-block"><div class="ssrcss-1o5p6v2-RichTextContainer e5tfeyi1"><p class="ssrcss-1q0x1qg-Paragraph e1jhz7w10">One of Trump's major lenders on his real estate projects is Deutsche Bank. </p><p class="ssrcss-1q0x1qg-Paragraph e1jhz7w10">The bank is <a class="ssrcss-f6h2dj-InlineLink e1kn3p7n0" href="/news/business-37605222">currently in negotiations</a> with the US justice department to settle a case involving misleading buyers when it sold mortgage bonds backed by risky loans.</p><p class="ssrcss-1q0x1qg-Paragraph e1jhz7w10"><b class="ssrcss-1xjjfut-BoldText e5tfeyi3">Update:</b> Deutsche Bank settled the mortgage bonds case for $7.2bn in late December 2016.</p></div></div><div class="ssrcss-10wcwg8-ComponentWrapper-FullWidthWrapper ep2nwvo1" data-component="image-block"><figure class="ssrcss-12gl1u2-StyledFigure e34k3c22"><div class="ssrcss-ab5fd8-StyledFigureContainer e34k3c21"><span class="ssrcss-ciorxc-Placeholder etlorgc0"><picture><source srcset="https://ichef.bbci.co.uk/ace/standard/240/mcs/media/images/75306000/jpg/_75306515_line976.jpg.webp 240w, https://ichef.bbci.co.uk/ace/standard/320/mcs/media/images/75306000/jpg/_75306515_line976.jpg 320w" width="464"/></picture></span></div></figure></div><div class="ssrcss-1o1fzgd-ComponentWrapper-HeadlineComponentWrapper egtrm1f0" data-component="subheadline-block"><h2 class="ssrcss-pbttu9-Heading e10rt3ze0" id="The-FCC" tabindex="-1"><span role="text">The FCC</span></h2></div><div class="ssrcss-suhx0k-RichTextComponentWrapper ep2nwvo0" data-component="text-block"><div class="ssrcss-1o5p6v2-RichTextContainer e5tfeyi1"><p class="ssrcss-1q0x1qg-Paragraph e1jhz7w10">The president has another job title beyond "commander-in-chief": executive producer. He will continue to have a "big stake" in The Celebrity Apprentice, which airs on NBC, linking Mr Trump's business interests with the network.</p><p class="ssrcss-1q0x1qg-Paragraph e1jhz7w10">NBC and its parent company, Comcast, is regulated by the Federal Communications Commission (FCC). Mr Trump's pick for the chairman, Ajit Pai, will be need to be reconfirmed by the Senate this year, in order to continue on at the commission.</p></div></div><div class="ssrcss-10wcwg8-ComponentWrapper-FullWidthWrapper ep2nwvo1" data-component="image-block"><figure class="ssrcss-12gl1u2-StyledFigure e34k3c22"><div class="ssrcss-ab5fd8-StyledFigureContainer e34k3c21"><span class="ssrcss-ciorxc-Placeholder etlorgc0"><picture><source srcset="https://ichef.bbci.co.uk/ace/standard/240/mcs/media/images/75306000/jpg/_75306515_line976.jpg.webp 240w, https://ichef.bbci.co.uk/ace/standard/320/mcs/media/images/75306000/jpg/_75306515_line976.jpg.webp 320w" type="image/webp"/><img alt="line" class="ssrcss-11yxrdo-Image edrdn950" height="2" loading="lazy" src="https://ichef.bbci.co.uk/ace/standard/464/mcs/media/images/75306000/jpg/_75306515_line976.jpg" srcset="https://ichef.bbci.co.uk/ace/standard/240/mcs/media/images/75306000/jpg/_75306515_line976.jpg 240w, https://ichef.bbci.co.uk/ace/standard/320/mcs/media/images/75306000/jpg/_75306515_line976.jpg 320w" width="464"/></picture></span></div></figure></div><div class="ssrcss-1o1fzgd-ComponentWrapper-HeadlineComponentWrapper egtrm1f0" data-component="subheadline-block"><h2 class="ssrcss-pbttu9-Heading e10rt3ze0" id="National-Labor-Relations-Board" tabindex="-1"><span role="text">National Labor Relations Board</span></h2></div><div class="ssrcss-suhx0k-RichTextComponentWrapper ep2nwvo0" data-component="text-block"><div class="ssrcss-1o5p6v2-RichTextContainer e5tfeyi1"><p class="ssrcss-1q0x1qg-Paragraph e1jhz7w10">On 3 November, the National Labor Relations Board (NLRB) ruled that Trump International Hotel Las Vegas - which Trump co-owns - <a class="ssrcss-f6h2dj-InlineLink e1kn3p7n0" href="https://www.nlrb.gov/case/28-CA-181475">broke the law by refusing to negotiate<span class="visually-hidden ssrcss-1f39n02-VisuallyHidden e16en2lz0">, <!-- -->external</span></a> with a hotel workers' union. </p><p class="ssrcss-1q0x1qg-Paragraph e1jhz7w10">The hotel appealed the case to a higher court. But three other labour disputes involving the Las Vegas hotel are currently before the board, as well as several others involving the Trump Organization.</p><p class="ssrcss-1q0x1qg-Paragraph e1jhz7w10">NLRB is facing an unprecedented situation on how to rule on disputes that will affect the president's business. Mr Trump has named current board member Philip Miscimarra as acting chair and will be able to appoint two new members to vacant spots.</p></div></div><div class="ssrcss-10wcwg8-ComponentWrapper-FullWidthWrapper ep2nwvo1" data-component="image-block"><figure class="ssrcss-12gl1u2-StyledFigure e34k3c22"><div class="ssrcss-ab5fd8-StyledFigureContainer e34k3c21"><span class="ssrcss-ciorxc-Placeholder etlorgc0"><picture><source srcset="https://ichef.bbci.co.uk/ace/standard/240/mcs/media/images/75306000/jpg/_75306515_line976.jpg.webp 240w, class="ssrcss-1o1fzgd-ComponentWrapper-HeadlineComponentWrapper egtrm1f0" data-component="subheadline-block"><h2 class="ssrcss-pbttu9-Heading e10rt3ze0" id="Secret-Service" tabindex="-1"><span role="text">Secret Service</span></h2></div><div class="ssrcss-10wcwg8-ComponentWrapper-FullWidthWrapper ep2nwvo1" data-component="image-block"><figure class="ssrcss-12gl1u2-StyledFigure role="text"><span class="visually-hidden ssrcss-1f39n02-VisuallyHidden e16en2lz0">Image source, </span>Reuters</span></div></figure></div><div class="ssrcss-suhx0k-RichTextComponentWrapper ep2nwvo0" data-component="text-block"><div class="ssrcss-1o5p6v2-RichTextContainer e5tfeyi1"><p class="ssrcss-1q0x1qg-Paragraph e1jhz7w10">During the campaign, Trump's airplane company, TAG Air, billed the Secret Service for flying on Trump's Boeing 757 while protecting the candidate. It is standard for Secret Service to pay their own way on private aircraft, and during the campaign, this was tracked by the Federal Election Commission through campaign finance reports.</p><p class="ssrcss-1q0x1qg-Paragraph e1jhz7w10">While Mr Trump flies on Air Force One and other US aircraft as president, if Trump or Pence family members are assigned protective detail and decide to fly on Trump planes, the Secret Service would need to reimburse TAG Air - and ultimately Mr Trump - for the flights. </p><p class="ssrcss-1q0x1qg-Paragraph e1jhz7w10">In addition, Secret Service <a class="ssrcss-f6h2dj-InlineLink e1kn3p7n0" href="http://www.cnn.com/2016/11/25/politics/secret-service-trump-tower/">will reportedly pay<span class="visually-hidden ssrcss-1f39n02-VisuallyHidden e16en2lz0">, <!-- -->external</span></a> the Trump Organization for the space they use in Trump Tower while protecting Melania and Barron Trump as they stay in New York for part of 2017. The Washington Post has reported the Secret Service has <a class="ssrcss-f6h2dj-InlineLink e1kn3p7n0" href="https://www.washingtonpost.com/politics/secret-service-asked-for-60-million-extra-for-trump-era-travel-and-protection-documents-show/2017/03/22/0967e7b6-0a85-11e7-a15f-a58d4a988474_story.html?utm_term=.b028c7bdaede">requested $27m extra<span class="visually-hidden ssrcss-1f39n02-VisuallyHidden e16en2lz0">, <!-- -->external</span></a> for the overall protective detail in New York.</p><p class="ssrcss-1q0x1qg-Paragraph e1jhz7w10">Secret Service has also paid to protect Eric Trump and Donald Trump Jr, as members of the president's family - even as they travel to take care of business for the Trump Organization.</p></div></div><div class="ssrcss-10wcwg8-ComponentWrapper-FullWidthWrapper ep2nwvo1" data-component="image-block"><figure class="ssrcss-12gl1u2-StyledFigure e34k3c22"><div class="ssrcss-ab5fd8-StyledFigureContainer e34k3c21"><span class="ssrcss-ciorxc-Placeholder etlorgc0"><picture><source srcset="https://ichef.bbci.co.uk/ace/standard/240/mcs/media/images/75306000/jpg/_75306515_line976.jpg.webp 240w, https://ichef.bbci.co.uk/ace/standard/320/mcs/media/images/75306000/jpg/_75306515_line976.jpg.webp 320w" type="image/webp"/><img alt="line" class="ssrcss-11yxrdo-Image edrdn950" height="2" loading="lazy" src="https://ichef.bbci.co.uk/ace/standard/464/mcs/media/images/75306000/jpg/_75306515_line976.jpg" srcset="https://ichef.bbci.co.uk/ace/standard/240/mcs/media/images/75306000/jpg/_75306515_line976.jpg 240w, https://ichef.bbci.co.uk/ace/standard/320/mcs/media/images/75306000/jpg/_75306515_line976.jpg 320w" width="464"/></picture></span></div></figure></div><div class="ssrcss-1o1fzgd-ComponentWrapper-HeadlineComponentWrapper egtrm1f0" data-component="subheadline-block"><h2 class="ssrcss-pbttu9-Heading e10rt3ze0" id="Stocks-" tabindex="-1"><span role="text">Stocks </span></h2></div><div class="ssrcss-suhx0k-RichTextComponentWrapper ep2nwvo0" data-component="text-block"><div class="ssrcss-1o5p6v2-RichTextContainer e5tfeyi1"><p class="ssrcss-1q0x1qg-Paragraph e1jhz7w10">Jason Miller, the transition team's spokesman, has said the president sold all his stocks in June 2016, a month after the required financial disclosure, but the campaign did not furnish proof nor provide an updated list of Mr Trump's investments.</p><p class="ssrcss-1q0x1qg-Paragraph e1jhz7w10">Since his election, Mr Trump has singled out specific companies for criticism on Twitter, causing price swings on the stock market. If Mr Trump still owns these stocks, he could make money off of selling and buying before and after such tweets.</p></div></div><div id="piano-inline2"></div><div class="ssrcss-10wcwg8-ComponentWrapper-FullWidthWrapper ep2nwvo1" data-component="image-block"><figure class="ssrcss-12gl1u2-StyledFigure e34k3c22"><div class="ssrcss-ab5fd8-StyledFigureContainer e34k3c21"><span class="ssrcss-ciorxc-Placeholder etlorgc0"><picture><source srcset="https://ichef.bbci.co.uk/ace/standard/240/mcs/media/images/75306000/jpg/_75306515_line976.jpg.webp 240w, https://ichef.bbci.co.uk/ace/standard/320/mcs/media/images/75306000/jpg/_75306515_line976.jpg.webp 320w" type="image/webp"/><img alt="line" class="ssrcss-11yxrdo-Image edrdn950" height="2" loading="lazy" src="https://ichef.bbci.co.uk/ace/standard/464/mcs/media/images/75306000/jpg/_75306515_line976.jpg" srcset="https://ichef.bbci.co.uk/ace/standard/240/mcs/media/images/75306000/jpg/_75306515_line976.jpg 240w, https://ichef.bbci.co.uk/ace/standard/320/mcs/media/images/75306000/jpg/_75306515_line976.jpg 320w" width="464"/></picture></span></div></figure></div><div class="ssrcss-1o1fzgd-ComponentWrapper-HeadlineComponentWrapper egtrm1f0" data-component="subheadline-block"><h2 class="ssrcss-pbttu9-Heading e10rt3ze0" id="Foreign-holdings" tabindex="-1"><span role="text">Foreign holdings</span></h2></div><div class="ssrcss-suhx0k-RichTextComponentWrapper ep2nwvo0" data-component="text-block"><div class="ssrcss-1o5p6v2-RichTextContainer e5tfeyi1"><p class="ssrcss-1q0x1qg-Paragraph e1jhz7w10">According to Trump's financial disclosure, as of mid-2016, he had investments in or owned companies in at least 20 countries. Unlike his domestic business, Mr Trump could run afoul of a clause in the US constitution by continuing to profit from these deals.</p><p class="ssrcss-1q0x1qg-Paragraph e1jhz7w10">The emoluments clause specifically prevents anyone who holds a US "office of trust or profit" from accepting gifts, payments or any benefit from a foreign nation.</p><p class="ssrcss-1q0x1qg-Paragraph e1jhz7w10">Even routine business benefits like tax breaks could violate the emoluments clause.</p><p class="ssrcss-1q0x1qg-Paragraph e1jhz7w10">One former White House ethics lawyer has <a class="ssrcss-f6h2dj-InlineLink e1kn3p7n0" href="http://www.rawstory.com/2016/11/former-bush-ethics-lawyer-trump-is-going-to-be-in-violation-of-the-constitution-on-day-1/">argued Mr Trump would be violation of the constitution<span class="visually-hidden ssrcss-1f39n02-VisuallyHidden e16en2lz0">, <!-- -->external</span></a> "on day one".</p><p class="ssrcss-1q0x1qg-Paragraph e1jhz7w10">In addition to emoluments, Mr Trump's foreign policy decisions could be called into question in any country in which the Trump Organization does business, especially when his policies would benefit the firm's holdings overseas.Here are some of Mr Trump's larger business deals that intersect with US foreign policy.</p><p class="ssrcss-1q0x1qg-Paragraph e1jhz7w10"><i class="ssrcss-xbdn93-ItalicText e5tfeyi2">BBC Monitoring contributed to this report</i></p></div></div><div class="ssrcss-10wcwg8-ComponentWrapper-FullWidthWrapper ep2nwvo1" data-component="image-block"><figure class="ssrcss-12gl1u2-StyledFigure e34k3c22"><div class="ssrcss-ab5fd8-StyledFigureContainer e34k3c21"><span class="ssrcss-ciorxc-Placeholder etlorgc0"><picture><source srcset="https://ichef.bbci.co.uk/ace/standard/240/cpsprodpb/D73B/production/_92699055_line976.jpg.webp 240w, class="ssrcss-1o1fzgd-ComponentWrapper-HeadlineComponentWrapper egtrm1f0" data-component="subheadline-block"><h2 class="ssrcss-pbttu9-Heading e10rt3ze0" id="Argentina" tabindex="-1"><span class="ssrcss-1q0x1qg-Paragraph e1jhz7w10">An Argentine broadcaster reported that Mr Trump allegedly asked President Mauricio Macri for his support to build an office tower in Buenos Aires while on call during Mr Trump's transition period. </p><p class="ssrcss-1q0x1qg-Paragraph e1jhz7w10">Mr Macri's office and the Trump campaign have denied the report. </p><p class="ssrcss-1q0x1qg-Paragraph e1jhz7w10">However, several days later, <a class="ssrcss-f6h2dj-InlineLink e1kn3p7n0" href="http://qz.com/843800/donald-trump-spoke-to-argentinas-president-then-three-days-later-his-associates-announced-trump-tower-buenos-aires-plans/">the Buenos Aires firm building the tower announced construction of the project was going ahead after years of delays<span class="visually-hidden ssrcss-1f39n02-VisuallyHidden e16en2lz0">, <!-- -->external</span></a>. </p></div></div><div class="ssrcss-10wcwg8-ComponentWrapper-FullWidthWrapper ep2nwvo1" data-component="image-block"><figure class="ssrcss-12gl1u2-StyledFigure e34k3c22"><div class="ssrcss-ab5fd8-StyledFigureContainer class="ssrcss-1o1fzgd-ComponentWrapper-HeadlineComponentWrapper egtrm1f0" data-component="subheadline-block"><h2 class="ssrcss-pbttu9-Heading e10rt3ze0" id="Brazil" tabindex="-1"><span role="text">Brazil</span></h2></div><div class="ssrcss-suhx0k-RichTextComponentWrapper ep2nwvo0" data-component="text-block"><div class="ssrcss-1o5p6v2-RichTextContainer e5tfeyi1"><p class="ssrcss-1q0x1qg-Paragraph e1jhz7w10">A waterfront property in Rio de Janeiro, branded with the Trump name through a licensing deal, is the subject of a federal inquiry after two small Brazilian pension funds invested heavily in the unfinished project, <a class="ssrcss-f6h2dj-InlineLink e1kn3p7n0" href="http://www.nytimes.com/2016/11/26/us/politics/donald-trump-international-business.html">with allegations of bribery<span class="visually-hidden ssrcss-1f39n02-VisuallyHidden e16en2lz0">, <!-- -->external</span></a>.</p><p class="ssrcss-1q0x1qg-Paragraph e1jhz7w10"><b class="ssrcss-1xjjfut-BoldText e5tfeyi3">Update: </b>The Trump Organization has reportedly cancelled <a class="ssrcss-f6h2dj-InlineLink e1kn3p7n0" href="http://bigstory.ap.org/article/b6ad7c24f59e491d9bfbfa24d540210a/trump-canceling-hotel-deal-azerbaijan-and-possibly-georgia">their licensing deal with the developers in Rio<span class="visually-hidden ssrcss-1f39n02-VisuallyHidden e16en2lz0">, <!-- -->external</span></a>. Trump lawyer Alan Garten told the AP in December this and a few other cancellations were "normal housekeeping" and not part of a strategy to reduce potential conflicts of interests.</p></div></div><div class="ssrcss-10wcwg8-ComponentWrapper-FullWidthWrapper ep2nwvo1" data-component="image-block"><figure class="ssrcss-12gl1u2-StyledFigure e34k3c22"><div srcset="https://ichef.bbci.co.uk/ace/standard/240/mcs/media/images/75306000/jpg/_75306515_line976.jpg.webp 240w, </span><div class="ssrcss-1ml6m0y-Stack e1y4nx260" spacing="6"><p class="ssrcss-1q0x1qg-Paragraph e1jhz7w10">Jared Kushner has a long list of things to do</p></div></figcaption></figure></div><div class="ssrcss-suhx0k-RichTextComponentWrapper ep2nwvo0" data-component="text-block"><div class="ssrcss-1o5p6v2-RichTextContainer e5tfeyi1"><p class="ssrcss-1q0x1qg-Paragraph e1jhz7w10">Meanwhile, Trump's son-in-law and now senior adviser, Jared Kushner, <a class="ssrcss-f6h2dj-InlineLink e1kn3p7n0" href="http://www.nytimes.com/aponline/2017/01/07/business/ap-us-trump-kushner.html">was negotiating a deal with China's Anbang Insurance Group<span class="visually-hidden ssrcss-1f39n02-VisuallyHidden e16en2lz0">, <!-- -->external</span></a> to redevelop 666 Fifth Avenue in New York City before <a class="ssrcss-f6h2dj-InlineLink e1kn3p7n0" href="http://www.reuters.com/article/us-usa-property-kushner-anbang-group-idUSKBN170224">backing out of talks in late March<span class="visually-hidden ssrcss-1f39n02-VisuallyHidden e16en2lz0">, <!-- -->external</span></a>.</p><p class="ssrcss-1q0x1qg-Paragraph e1jhz7w10">Mr Kushner has been given a senior role inside the White House. His lawyer <a class="ssrcss-f6h2dj-InlineLink e1kn3p7n0" href="http://www.nytimes.com/2016/09/02/world/asia/china-anbang-insurance.html">told the New York Times<span class="visually-hidden ssrcss-1f39n02-VisuallyHidden e16en2lz0">, <!-- -->external</span></a> he "would recuse from particular matters that would have a direct and predictable effect on his remaining financial interests" without giving specifics.</p><p class="ssrcss-1q0x1qg-Paragraph e1jhz7w10">Ivanka Trump, who has her own non-paying position at the White House, has advised her father on a broad number of policy areas, including high-profile foreign policy meetings.</p><p class="ssrcss-1q0x1qg-Paragraph e1jhz7w10">On the same day she sat next to Chinese President at a dinner at Mar-a-Lago, the Chinese government approved <a class="ssrcss-f6h2dj-InlineLink e1kn3p7n0" href="https://apnews.com/d9e34f23a64947d99e4a7d757012c509?utm_campaign=SocialFlow&amp;utm_source=Twitter&amp;utm_medium=AP">three new trademarks for Ms Trump's firm<span class="visually-hidden ssrcss-1f39n02-VisuallyHidden e16en2lz0">, <!-- -->external</span></a> to sell items in China.</p><p class="ssrcss-1q0x1qg-Paragraph e1jhz7w10">While Ms Trump has moved her firm to a trust and said she will not partake in decisions could led to conflicts, ethics experts are concerned with the broadening scope of both her business, which bears her name, and her advisory role at the White House.</p></div></div><div id="piano-inline3"></div><div class="ssrcss-10wcwg8-ComponentWrapper-FullWidthWrapper ep2nwvo1" class="ssrcss-1q0x1qg-Paragraph e1jhz7w10">The firm with developers of a beachfront planned community but the project stalled, and Trump sued in 2012 for unpaid licencing fees.</p><p class="ssrcss-1q0x1qg-Paragraph e1jhz7w10">But in February, owners made a show of <a class="ssrcss-f6h2dj-InlineLink e1kn3p7n0" href="http://capcana.com/news/cap-cana-welcomes-eric-trump/">announcing Eric Trump<span class="visually-hidden ssrcss-1f39n02-VisuallyHidden e16en2lz0">, <!-- -->external</span></a> had toured the project, saying "we are excited to be working with the Trump Organization in the future phases of the project".</p><p class="ssrcss-1q0x1qg-Paragraph e1jhz7w10">A Trump Organization lawyer has described the deal as "never dead" and said discussions were "very preliminary" but some investors were surprised to find the firm was still technically involved in the project.</p></div></div><div class="ssrcss-10wcwg8-ComponentWrapper-FullWidthWrapper ep2nwvo1" -->external</span></a>.</p><p class="ssrcss-1q0x1qg-Paragraph e1jhz7w10">In addition, one of Trump's advisers, Carl Icahn, is a major shareholder of Freeport, which is looking to extend a mining Like many of Trump's branding projects, Mr Trump does not own the building himself, but licenses his name to the building in return for regular payments.</p><p class="ssrcss-1q0x1qg-Paragraph e1jhz7w10">Trump family members have previously promoted the project, including a promotional video. </p><p class="ssrcss-1q0x1qg-Paragraph e1jhz7w10">The trade envoy/business partner reportedly flew to US to hold a private meeting with Mr Trump <a class="ssrcss-f6h2dj-InlineLink e1kn3p7n0" href="http://www.nytimes.com/2016/11/26/us/politics/donald-trump-international-business.html">after the election<span class="visually-hidden ssrcss-1f39n02-VisuallyHidden e16en2lz0">, <!-- -->external</span></a>. </p></div></div><div class="ssrcss-10wcwg8-ComponentWrapper-FullWidthWrapper ep2nwvo1" The Taoyan mayor's office said the woman had "authorisation documents" but did not specify what kind, <a class="ssrcss-f6h2dj-InlineLink e1kn3p7n0" href="http://www.nytimes.com/2016/12/04/world/asia/taiwan-city-planning-makeover-says-trump-agent-showed-interest.html">the New York Times reported<span class="visually-hidden ssrcss-1f39n02-VisuallyHidden e16en2lz0">, <!-- -->external</span></a>.</p><p class="ssrcss-1q0x1qg-Paragraph e1jhz7w10">A month after his election, Trump called the president of Taiwan directly, <a class="ssrcss-f6h2dj-InlineLink e1kn3p7n0" href="/news/world-asia-china-38218202">breaking decades of existing US foreign policy</a>.
